<h2 class="mume-header" id="function-i">Function i</h2>

<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msup><mi>x</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msup><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>d</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi><msup><mrow></mrow><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">&#x2032;</mo></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>3</mn><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><msup><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi><msup><mrow></mrow><mrow><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo></mrow></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi>x</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><msub><mi>b</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
    f_{i}(x) &amp;= a_{i}x^{3} + b_{i}x^{2} + c_{i}x + d_{i} \\

<h2 class="mume-header" id="constrains">Constrains</h2>

<p><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">&#x2200;</mi><mi>i</mi><mo>&#x2208;</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>&#x2026;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\forall i \in \{2 \ldots n-1\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.73354em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord">&#x2200;</span><span class="mord mathdefault">i</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&#x2208;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="minner">&#x2026;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathdefault">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">&#x2212;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span>:<br>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi><msup><mrow></mrow><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">&#x2032;</mo></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&#x2212;</mo><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>&#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msup><mrow></mrow><mo mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">&#x2032;</mo></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi><msup><mrow></mrow><mrow><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo></mrow></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&#x2212;</mo><msubsup><mi>f</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>&#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><msup><mrow></mrow><mrow><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo><mo mathvariant="normal">&#x2032;</mo></mrow></msup></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
    f_{i}(x_{i}) - f_{i-1}(x_{i}) &amp;= 0 \\
    f^{&apos;}_{i}(x_{i}) - f^{&apos;}_{i-1}(x_{i}) &amp;= 0 \\
    f^{&apos;&apos;}_{i}(x_{i}) - f^{&apos;&apos;}_{i-1}(x_{i}) &amp;= 0
    \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" <h2 class="mume-header" id="cost-function">Cost Function</h2>

<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.24999999999999992em" columnalign="right     F_{i} &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}f_i &amp; f_i^{&apos;} &amp; f_i^{&apos;&apos;}\end{bmatrix}^{T} \\
    Y_{i} &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}y_i &amp; y_i^{&apos;} &amp; y_i^{&apos;&apos;}\end{bmatrix}^{T} \\
    E_i^j &amp;= F_i(x_j) - Y_j \\
    g_i^1 &amp;= f_{i}(x_{i}) - f_{i-1}(x_{i}) \\
    g_i^2 &amp;= f^{&apos;}_{i}(x_{i}) - f^{&apos;}_{i-1}(x_{i}) \\
    g_i^3 &amp;= f^{&apos;&apos;}_{i}(x_{i}) - f^{&apos;&apos;}_{i-1}(x_{i}) \\
    g_i &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}g_i^1 &amp; g_i^2 &amp; g_i^3\end{bmatrix}^{T} \\
    g_1 &amp;=  f_1^{&apos;&apos;}(x_1) \\
    g_n &amp;=  f_{n-1}^{&apos;&apos;}(x_n) \\
    \phi_{i} &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}\phi_i^1 &amp; \phi_i^2 &amp; \phi_i^3\end{bmatrix}^{T}
    \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut"     H = \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X^2} = \frac{\partial }{\partial X}(\frac{\partial O}{\partial X}) =
        \begin{bmatrix}
            \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_1^2} &amp; \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_1\partial X_2} &amp; \ldots &amp; \frac{\partial O}{\partial X_1\partial X_m} \\
            \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_2\partial X_1} &amp; \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_2^2} &amp; \ldots &amp; \frac{\partial O}{\partial X_2\partial X_m} \\
            \vdots &amp; \vdots &amp; \ddots &amp;\vdots \\
            \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_m\partial X_1} &amp; \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_m\partial X_2} &amp; \ldots &amp; \frac{\partial^2 O}{\partial X_m^2}
        \end{bmatrix}
    \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
    B &amp;= -\left.\frac{\partial O}{\partial X}\right| _{X=0} \\
    B &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}
        B_1^{\phi} &amp; B_1^{\beta} &amp; B_2^{\phi} &amp; B_2^{\beta} &amp; \ldots &amp; B_{n-1}^{\phi} &amp; B_{n-1}^{\beta} &amp; B_n^{\phi}
        \end{bmatrix}^T \\
    B_i^{\phi} &amp;= -\left.\frac{\partial O}{\partial \phi_i}\right| _{\phi_i=0} = 0 \\
    B_i^{\beta} &amp;= -\left.\frac{\partial O}{\partial \beta_i}\right| _{\beta_i=0} = \begin{bmatrix}
        2w_1(y_ix_i^3 + y_{i+1}x_{i+1}^3) + 6w_2(y_i^{&apos;}x_i^2 + y_{i+1}^{&apos;}x_{i+1}^2) + 12w_3(y_i^{&apos;&apos;}x_i + y_{i+1}^{&apos;&apos;}x_{i+1}) \\
        2w_1(y_ix_i^2 + y_{i+1}x_{i+1}^2) + 4w_2(y_i^{&apos;}x_i + y_{i+1}^{&apos;}x_{i+1}) + 4w_3(y_i^{&apos;&apos;} + y_{i+1}^{&apos;&apos;}) \\
        2w_1(y_ix_i + y_{i+1}x_{i+1}) + 2w_2(y_i^{&apos;} + y_{i+1}^{&apos;}) \\
        2w_1(y_i + y_{i+1})
        \end{bmatrix}
    \end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" <h2 class="mume-header" id="form-of-h-matrix">Form of H Matrix</h2>

    A_i^{11} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^6+x_{i+1}^6)+18w_2(x_i^4+x_{i+1}^4)+72w_3(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2) \\
    A_i^{12} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^5+x_{i+1}^5)+12w_2(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3)+24w_3(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    A_i^{13} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^4+x_{i+1}^4)+6w_2(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2) \\
    A_i^{14} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3) \\
    \\
    A_i^{21} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^5+x_{i+1}^5)+12w_2(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3)+24w_3(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    A_i^{22} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^4+x_{i+1}^4)+8w_2(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2)+16w_3 \\
    A_i^{23} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3)+4w_2(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    A_i^{24} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2) \\
    \\
    A_i^{31} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^4+x_{i+1}^4)+6w_2(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2) \\
    A_i^{32} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3)+4w_2(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    A_i^{33} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2)+4w_2 \\
    A_i^{34} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    \\
    A_i^{41} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^3+x_{i+1}^3) \\
    A_i^{42} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i^2+x_{i+1}^2) \\
    A_i^{43} &amp;= 2w_1(x_i+x_{i+1}) \\
    A_i^{44} &amp;= 4w_1 \\
    \\
    T_i &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}
        x_i^3 &amp; 3x_i^2 &amp; 6x_i \\
        x_i^2 &amp; 2x_i &amp; 2 \\
        x_i &amp; 1 &amp; 0 \\
        1 &amp; 0 &amp; 0
        \end{bmatrix} \\
    T_1 &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}
        6x_1 &amp; 2 &amp;0 &amp; 0
        \end{bmatrix}^T \\
    T_n &amp;= \begin{bmatrix}
        6x_n &amp; 2 &amp;0 &amp; 0
        \end{bmatrix}^T
